# Description_Notes_and_Keywords
#   Description: WALD-WASSER-WEINviertel collection of living oak and pine tree data, eastern Austria. Regional multi-species collection from ~48.27N - 48.68N, 15.82E-16.88N, ~220m elevation.  Species include Pinus nigra J.F. Arnold, Pinus sylvestris L., Quercus cerris L., Quercus petraea (Matt.) Liebl., and Quercus robur L.   Sample ID's, e.g. AbcXY07m, are composed of Abc=abbreviation for site, XY=abbreviation for species.  (PN = Pinus nigra, PS = Pinus sylvestris, QC = Quercus cerris, QS = Quercus robur or Q. petraea), 07=number of tree at this site, m=mean of two or more cores per tree (can also be a, b, c for single cores) NOAA Template Raw Measurements file added 2019-02-05.
